{
  "replace_all": false,
  "file_path": "<AWS_SECRET_REDACTED>ns/system-health-dashboard/src/components/workflow/multi-agent-graph.tsx",
  "old_string": "      // Collapse when: all substeps completed AND we've shown them as green for at least 500ms\n      // This ensures the user sees the completed state before collapse\n      const completedLongEnough = agentCompletedTimeRef.current &&\n        (Date.now() - agentCompletedTimeRef.current) >= 500\n\n      if (wasAutoExpanded && allSubstepsCompleted && differentStepRunning && completedLongEnough) {\n        setExpandedSubStepsAgent(null)\n        setAutoExpandedAgent(null)\n        agentCompletedTimeRef.current = null\n      }\n    }\n  }, [effectiveSteps, expandedSubStepsAgent, autoExpandedAgent, stepToAgent, effectiveAgentSubSteps])",
  "new_string": "      // Collapse when: all substeps completed AND we've shown them as green for at least 500ms\n      // This ensures the user sees the completed state before collapse\n      const COLLAPSE_DELAY_MS = 500\n      const completedLongEnough = agentCompletedTimeRef.current &&\n        (Date.now() - agentCompletedTimeRef.current) >= COLLAPSE_DELAY_MS\n\n      if (wasAutoExpanded && allSubstepsCompleted && differentStepRunning && completedLongEnough) {\n        setExpandedSubStepsAgent(null)\n        setAutoExpandedAgent(null)\n        agentCompletedTimeRef.current = null\n      } else if (wasAutoExpanded && allSubstepsCompleted && differentStepRunning && !completedLongEnough) {\n        // Schedule a re-check after the delay to trigger collapse\n        const remainingTime = COLLAPSE_DELAY_MS - (Date.now() - (agentCompletedTimeRef.current || Date.now()))\n        const timer = setTimeout(() => {\n          setExpandedSubStepsAgent(null)\n          setAutoExpandedAgent(null)\n          agentCompletedTimeRef.current = null\n        }, Math.max(remainingTime, 50))\n        return () => clearTimeout(timer)\n      }\n    }\n  }, [effectiveSteps, expandedSubStepsAgent, autoExpandedAgent, stepToAgent, effectiveAgentSubSteps])"

### Edit - 2026-01-30 08:54:18 UTC [09:54:18 CEST]

**User Request:** This made it worse - now the sub-steps don't show in free-flying mode on KG-Ops and the last step sometimes doesn't get made active (dark blue) & completed (green) before switching away. This could be async, if the WF has jumped away by then and it is just a lagging display that should be completed for clarity

**Tool:** Edit
**Input:** ```json
{
  "replace_all": false,
  "file_path": "<AWS_SECRET_REDACTED>ns/system-health-dashboard/src/components/workflow/multi-agent-graph.tsx",
  "old_string": "      // Collapse when: all substeps completed AND we've shown them as green for at least 500ms\n      // This ensures the user sees the completed state before collapse\n      const completedLongEnough = agentCompletedTimeRef.current &&\n        (Date.now() - agentCompletedTimeRef.current) >= 500\n\n      if (wasAutoExpanded && allSubstepsCompleted && differentStepRunning && completedLongEnough) {\n        setExpandedSubStepsAgent(null)\n        setAutoExpandedAgent(null)\n        agentCompletedTimeRef.current = null\n      }\n    }\n  }, [effectiveSteps, expandedSubStepsAgent, autoExpandedAgent, stepToAgent, effectiveAgentSubSteps])",
  "new_string": "      // Collapse when: all substeps completed AND we've shown them as green for at least 500ms\n      // This ensures the user sees the completed state before collapse\n      const COLLAPSE_DELAY_MS = 500\n      const completedLongEnough = agentCompletedTimeRef.current &&\n        (Date.now() - agentCompletedTimeRef.current) >= COLLAPSE_DELAY_MS\n\n      if (wasAutoExpanded && allSubstepsCompleted && differentStepRunning && completedLongEnough) {\n        setExpandedSubStepsAgent(null)\n        setAutoExpandedAgent(null)\n        agentCompletedTimeRef.current = null\n      } else if (wasAutoExpanded && allSubstepsCompleted && differentStepRunning && !completedLongEnough) {\n        // Schedule a re-check after the delay to trigger collapse\n        const remainingTime = COLLAPSE_DELAY_MS - (Date.now() - (agentCompletedTimeRef.current || Date.now()))\n        const timer = setTimeout(() => {\n          setExpandedSubStepsAgent(null)\n          setAutoExpandedAgent(null)\n          agentCompletedTimeRef.current = null\n        }, Math.max(remainingTime, 50))\n        return () => clearTimeout(timer)\n      }\n    }\n  }, [effectiveSteps, expandedSubStepsAgent, autoExpandedAgent, stepToAgent, effectiveAgentSubSteps])"
}
